# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

Use `sg_list_repos` to discover available repositories before searching.


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

# Firefox CSS Style Resolution to Layout Paint Chain

## Your Task

Trace how a CSS style change triggers layout and paint in mozilla/gecko-dev. Find C++ source files implementing: the style change notification, the frame style recomputation, the dirty-frame reflow scheduling, the display list construction, and the WebRender layer update.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/firefox--871325b8.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/firefox--871325b8` (mozilla-firefox/firefox)

```json
}
```

77-assistanttext-
Perfect! I've successfully traced the CSS style resolution to layout and paint chain in mozilla/gecko-dev and created a comprehensive answer file. Here's a summary of what I found:

## The Complete CSS Style-to-Paint Chain

**1. Style Change Notification** (layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp)
- `PostRestyleEvent()` initiates the process
- Calls `Servo_NoteExplicitHints()` to notify the Servo style engine

**2. Frame Style Recomputation** (layout/style/ServoStyleSet.cpp)
- ServoStyleSet manages style computation across the DOM tree
- RestyleManager coordinates the restyling process

**3. Dirty-Frame Reflow Scheduling** (layout/base/PresShell.cpp)
- `FrameNeedsReflow()` marks frames as dirty (NS_FRAME_IS_DIRTY or NS_FRAME_HAS_DIRTY_CHILDREN)
- `DoReflow()` performs the actual layout reflow
- `SchedulePaint()` schedules rendering updates

**4. Display List Construction** (layout/painting/)
- `RetainedDisplayListBuilder` incrementally builds display lists
- `nsDisplayListBuilder` constructs complete display lists from frame hierarchies
- `PaintInternal()` orchestrates the painting process

**5. WebRender Layer Update** (gfx/layers/wr/)
- `WebRenderCommandBuilder::CreateWebRenderCommands()` converts display items to WebRender commands
- `RenderRootStateManager` manages WebRender state
- Commands are sent to GPU for final rendering

The answer file at `/workspace/answer.json` contains all relevant C++ source files, key symbols, and a detailed narrative explaining the complete flow.

This function records the style change and calls `Servo_NoteExplicitHints()` to notify the Servo style engine.\\n\\n**Frame style recomputation** is managed by `layout/style/ServoStyleSet.cpp`, which contains the ServoStyleSet class. This component orchestrates the style computation across the DOM tree using Servo's style engine. The RestyleManager coordinates this process and maintains state about which elements need restyling via `layout/style/RestyleManager.cpp`.\\n\\nOnce styles are recomputed, the **dirty-frame reflow scheduling** occurs through `layout/base/PresShell.cpp:FrameNeedsReflow()`. After reflow, `layout/base/PresShell.cpp:PaintInternal()` orchestrates the painting process and display list generation.\\n\\nFinally, **WebRender layer updates** are performed through `gfx/layers/wr/WebRenderCommandBuilder.cpp`. The `CreateWebRenderCommands()` and `CreateWebRenderCommandsFromDisplayList()` functions convert display items into WebRender drawing commands. The `gfx/layers/wr/RenderRootStateManager.cpp:RenderRootStateManager` class manages the WebRender state for each render root. These commands are then sent to the WebRender engine via `gfx/layers/wr/WebRenderLayerManager.h` and the WebRender bridge, ultimately resulting in the GPU rendering the updated visual content.\\n\\nThe entire chain ensures that CSS style changes trigger a coordinated sequence of operations: style recomputation \u2192 dirty frame marking \u2192 layout reflow \u2192 display list construction \u2192 WebRender layer updates \u2192 GPU rendering.\"\n}\n",
